#### What this PR does / why we need it:
Feature LendingLimit provides a guaranteed resource quota for user.
#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:
<!--
*Automatically closes linked issue when PR is merged.
Usage: `Fixes #<issue number>`, or `Fixes (paste link of issue)`.
_If PR is about `failing-tests or flakes`, please post the related issues/tests in a comment and do not use `Fixes`_*

#1224
[KEP-1224](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1331)

#### Special notes for your reviewer:

#### Does this PR introduce a user-facing change?
<!--
If no, just write "NONE" in the release-note block below.
If yes, a release note is required:
Enter your extended release note in the block below. If the PR requires additional action from users switching to the new release, include the string "action required".
-->
```release-note
Add a lendingLimit field in ClusterQueue's quotas, to allow restricting how much of the unused resources by the ClusterQueue can be borrowed by other ClusterQueues in the cohort.
In other words, this allows a quota equal to `nominal-lendingLimit` to be exclusively used by the ClusterQueue.
```

### Comment by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2023-12-04T10:53:12Z

Just to confirm, here I have 2 cqs and 2 rfs.
In the first case, set  `whenCanBorrow` to `Borrow`(default)
cq-a.yaml:
```
apiVersion: kueue.x-k8s.io/v1beta1
kind: ClusterQueue
metadata:
  name: "cq-a"
spec:
  namespaceSelector: {} # match all.
  cohort: "cohort-ab"
  resourceGroups:
  - coveredResources: ["cpu"]
    flavors:
    - name: "arm"
      resources:
      - name: "cpu"
        nominalQuota: 500m
    - name: "x86"
      resources:
      - name: "cpu"
        nominalQuota: 600m
  flavorFungibility:
    whenCanBorrow: Borrow
```
cq-b.yaml:
```
apiVersion: kueue.x-k8s.io/v1beta1
kind: ClusterQueue
metadata:
  name: "cq-b"
spec:
  namespaceSelector: {} # match all.
  cohort: "cohort-ab"
  resourceGroups:
  - coveredResources: ["cpu"]
    flavors:
    - name: "arm"
      resources:
      - name: "cpu"
        nominalQuota: 300m
        lendingLimit: 100m
    - name: "x86"
      resources:
      - name: "cpu"
        nominalQuota: 200m
        lendingLimit: 0m
```
Then a workload with `600m` cpu request to lq-a(belongs to cq-a) with the flavor `arm`(or `x86`) should be admitted and assigned to the flavor it requested, but `700m` shouldn't, right?

And in the second case, set  `whenCanBorrow` to `TryNextFlavor`.
A workload with `600m` cpu request to lq-a with the flavor `arm` should be admitted and assigned to the flavor `x86`.

In conclusion, I just want to make sure that: Borrow(or Lend) can only happen in the same flavor(like, horizontal?), right?
If there's only 1 cq and 2 rf:
```
  - coveredResources: ["cpu"]
    flavors:
    - name: "arm"
      resources:
      - name: "cpu"
        nominalQuota: 500m
    - name: "x86"
      resources:
      - name: "cpu"
        nominalQuota: 600m
        lendingLimit: 100m
```
Then Borrow(or Lend) should not work in different flavor(like, vertical?), right?

If that so, I'm going to modify KEP-1224 in [Integration tests](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/main/keps/1224-lending-limit/README.md#integration-tests) like this:

- In a cohort with 2 ClusterQueues cq-a, cq-b and 2 ResourceFlavors rf-a, rf-b:
  - In cq-b, when rf-a's LendingLimit set, and cq-a's FlavorFungibility set to `whenCanBorrow: Borrow`:
    - In cq-a, when rf-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `rf-a's LendingLimit`.
    - In cq-a, when rf-a's BorrowingLimit set, cq-a can borrow as much as `min(rf-a's LendingLimit, rf-a's BorrowingLimit)`.
  - In cq-b, when rf-b's LendingLimit set, and cq-a's FlavorFungibility set to `whenCanBorrow: TryNextFlavor`:
    - In cq-a, when rf-b's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `rf-b's LendingLimit`.
    - In cq-a, when rf-b's BorrowingLimit set, cq-a can borrow as much as `min(rf-b's LendingLimit, rf-b's BorrowingLimit)`.

### Comment by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2023-12-04T10:57:18Z

> In conclusion, I just want to make sure that: Borrow(or Lend) can only happen in the same flavor(like, horizontal?), right?
> Borrow(or Lend) should not work in different flavor(like, vertical?), right?

@tenzen-y Hi! Sorry to bother, but am I understanding correctly?

### Comment by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2023-12-05T02:49:47Z

> Then a workload with 600m cpu request to lq-a(belongs to cq-a) with the flavor arm(or x86) should be admitted and assigned to the flavor it requested, but 700m shouldn't, right?

@B1F030 If there are no admitted workloads, the workload should be assigned to arm flavor since the flavors are evaluated in order. Also, as you say, workloads with 700m CPU requests wouldn't admitted by any clusterQueue.

> And in the second case, set whenCanBorrow to TryNextFlavor.
A workload with 600m cpu request to lq-a with the flavor arm should be admitted and assigned to the flavor x86.

If the workload doesn't have a nodeSelector for the arm flavor, it's correct.

> In conclusion, I just want to make sure that: Borrow(or Lend) can only happen in the same flavor(like, horizontal?), right?

Yes, the Borrow will affect only the same flavors of each resource, like CPU. A workload can have only a single flavor of each resource. In other words, a workload can not have multiple flavors against a single resource, although a workload can have multiple flavors with multiple resources.

It means `cpu=flavor-a and memory=flavor-b` will happen, although `cpu=flavor-a and flavor-b` won't happen.

### Comment by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2023-12-05T04:25:38Z

> Yes, the Borrow will affect only the same flavors of each resource, like CPU. A workload can have only a single flavor of each resource. In other words, a workload can not have multiple flavors against a single resource, although a workload can have multiple flavors with multiple resources.

Thanks a lot!

## Reviews

### Review by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) (commented) — 2023-12-07T09:50:07Z

The preemption file not checked yet.

Please append the commit not squash them, thanks.

- **apis/kueue/v1beta1/clusterqueue_types.go:201** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2023-12-07T07:08:29Z
```diff
@@ -194,13 +194,23 @@ type ResourceQuota struct {
 	// combination that this ClusterQueue is allowed to borrow from the unused
 	// quota of other ClusterQueues in the same cohort.
 	// In total, at a given time, Workloads in a ClusterQueue can consume a
-	// quantity of quota equal to nominalQuota+borrowingLimit, assuming the other
+	// quantity of quota equals to nominalQuota+borrowingLimit, assuming the other
 	// ClusterQueues in the cohort have enough unused quota.
 	// If null, it means that there is no borrowing limit.
 	// If not null, it must be non-negative.
 	// borrowingLimit must be null if spec.cohort is empty.
```

  I'm challenging why this is necessary, we can ignore the borrowingLimit as well as lendingLimit when cohort is empty(and actually we don't need to change any code I guess) Under some circumstances, like transmit from `both set borrowingLimit and cohort` to `set the cohort to empty` for temporary interrupt resource sharing, we no longer need to modify the borrowingLimit.

- **keps/1224-lending-limit/README.md:150** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2023-12-07T07:21:55Z

```diff
@@ -144,9 +144,12 @@ After the implementation PR is merged, add the names of the tests here.
     - When cq-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `(cq-b's LendingLimit + cq-c's LendingLimit)`.
     - When cq-a's BorrowingLimit set, cq-a can borrow as much as `min((cq-b's LendingLimit + cq-c's LendingLimit), cq-a's BorrowingLimit)`.
 - In a cohort with 2 ClusterQueues cq-a, cq-b and 2 ResourceFlavors rf-a, rf-b:
-  - When rf-b's LendingLimit set, and cq-a's FlavorFungibility set to `WhenCanBorrow: TryNextFlavor`:
-    - When rf-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `rf-b's LendingLimit`.
-    - When rf-a's BorrowingLimit set, cq-a can borrow as much as `min(rf-b's LendingLimit, rf-a's BorrowingLimit)`.
+  - In cq-b, when rf-a's LendingLimit set, and cq-a's FlavorFungibility set to `whenCanBorrow: Borrow`:
+    - In cq-a, when rf-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `rf-a's LendingLimit`.
```

  I'm confusing here, if we set the `FlavorFungibility` to cq-a, then we should test borrowing resources from cq-b, then this should be rf-b's lendingLimit?

```diff
 				available := cohortResources[resource] - cohortUsage[resource]
+				// if LendingLimit enabled, we need to recalculate cohort.RequestableResources
```

### Review by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) (commented) — 2023-12-07T10:09:30Z

- **keps/1224-lending-limit/README.md:150** by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2023-12-07T10:09:29Z
```diff
@@ -144,9 +144,12 @@ After the implementation PR is merged, add the names of the tests here.
     - When cq-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `(cq-b's LendingLimit + cq-c's LendingLimit)`.
     - When cq-a's BorrowingLimit set, cq-a can borrow as much as `min((cq-b's LendingLimit + cq-c's LendingLimit), cq-a's BorrowingLimit)`.
 - In a cohort with 2 ClusterQueues cq-a, cq-b and 2 ResourceFlavors rf-a, rf-b:
-  - When rf-b's LendingLimit set, and cq-a's FlavorFungibility set to `WhenCanBorrow: TryNextFlavor`:
-    - When rf-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `rf-b's LendingLimit`.
-    - When rf-a's BorrowingLimit set, cq-a can borrow as much as `min(rf-b's LendingLimit, rf-a's BorrowingLimit)`.
+  - In cq-b, when rf-a's LendingLimit set, and cq-a's FlavorFungibility set to `whenCanBorrow: Borrow`:
+    - In cq-a, when rf-a's BorrowingLimit unset, cq-a can borrow as much as `rf-a's LendingLimit`.
```

  cq-a:
  ```
      flavors:
      - name: "rf-a"
          nominalQuota
      - name: "rf-b"
          nominalQuota
    flavorFungibility:
      whenCanBorrow: Borrow
  ```
  cq-b:
  ```
      flavors:
      - name: "rf-a"
          nominalQuota
          lendingLimit
      - name: "rf-b"
          nominalQuota
          lendingLimit
  ```
  `whenCanBorrow: Borrow`: cq-a's rf-a borrow from cq-b's rf-a
  `whenCanBorrow: TryNextFlavor`: cq-a's rf-b borrow from cq-b's rf-b

- **pkg/scheduler/preemption/preemption.go:376** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-02T06:16:31Z
```diff
@@ -336,14 +337,42 @@ func workloadFits(wlReq cache.FlavorResourceQuantities, cq *cache.ClusterQueue,
 				cohortResRequestable = cq.Cohort.RequestableResources[flvQuotas.Name]
 			}
 			for rName, rReq := range flvReq {
+				flagBorrow, flagLend := false, false
 				limit := flvQuotas.Resources[rName].Nominal
+				if !allowBorrowing || cq.Cohort == nil {
+					if cqResUsage[rName]+rReq > limit {
+						return false
+					}
+				}
 
 				// No need to check whether cohort is nil here because when borrowingLimit
 				// is non nil, cohort is always non nil.
 				if allowBorrowing && flvQuotas.Resources[rName].BorrowingLimit != nil {
+					flagBorrow = true
 					limit += *flvQuotas.Resources[rName].BorrowingLimit
+					if cqResUsage[rName]+rReq > limit {
+						return false
+					}
 				}
 
+				// TODO: add validation for lendingLimit in cohort
+				if allowBorrowing && cq.Cohort != nil && features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+					if flvQuotas.Resources[rName].LendingLimit != nil {
+						flagLend = true
+						// If LendingLimit is not nil here, we need to recalculate cohort.RequestableResources,
+						// because we are borrowing from the cohort now, need to count our own nominal quota in.
+						if guarantee, exist := cq.GetGuaranteedQuota(flvQuotas.Name, rName); exist {
+							cohortResRequestable[rName] += guarantee
+						}
+					}
+				}
+				if flagBorrow && flagLend {
+					// if lendingLimit and borrowingLimit both set
+					limit = min(cohortResRequestable[rName], limit)
+				} else {
+					// if one of lendingLimit and borrowingLimit unset
+					limit = max(cohortResRequestable[rName], limit)
+				}
 				if cqResUsage[rName]+rReq > limit {
```

  Based on my understanding, what we need is only change L380:L82 to:
  ```
  if cq.Cohort != nil {
      requestQuota :=  cohortResRequestable[rName]
      if lendingLimit != nil {
          requestQuota += guarantee
      }
  
      if cohortResUsage[rName]+rReq > requestQuota {
          return false
      }
  }
  ```
  
  Then we can make sure  that the borrowing resources will not exceed.

```diff
@@ -180,6 +182,13 @@ func validateFlavorQuotas(flavorQuotas kueue.FlavorQuotas, coveredResources []co
 			allErrs = append(allErrs, validateResourceQuantity(*rq.BorrowingLimit, borrowingLimitPath)...)
 			allErrs = append(allErrs, validateBorrowingLimit(*rq.BorrowingLimit, cohort, borrowingLimitPath)...)
 		}
+		if features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) && rq.LendingLimit != nil {
+			lendingLimitPath := path.Child("lendingLimit")
+			allErrs = append(allErrs, validateResourceQuantity(*rq.LendingLimit, lendingLimitPath)...)
+			// LendingLimit must be nil when cohort is empty
+			allErrs = append(allErrs, validateBorrowingLimit(*rq.LendingLimit, cohort, lendingLimitPath)...)
```

  No, just reusing the same function as BorrowingLimit to validate, make sure the LendingLimit be nil when cohort is empty.

```diff
+				if features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {

```

- **pkg/cache/snapshot.go:204** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2024-01-16T18:02:15Z

```diff
 		}
 	}
 }
+
+// RequestableQuota recalculates cohort.RequestableResources when LendingLimit enabled,
+// because when borrowing from the cohort, need to count cq's own nominal quota in.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
```

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:129** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2024-01-16T18:14:41Z
```diff
@@ -120,12 +126,12 @@ func newCohort(name string, size int) *Cohort {
 	}
 }
 
-func (c *Cohort) CanFit(q FlavorResourceQuantities) bool {
+func (c *ClusterQueue) FitInCohort(q FlavorResourceQuantities) bool {
```

  I don't think this logic is right. Assume the following:
  
  ```
  CQ A:
    nominal: 2
    lendingLimit: 2
    workloads: <empty>
  
  CQ B:
    nominal: 3
    lendingLimit: 2
     workloads: {2} // one workload consuming 2 units
  ```
  
  Next, there is an incoming workload of size 3. This should fit by using 2 free units in CQ A, and one free unit in CQ B (it's under the lending limit).
  
  However, with the current implementation, `RequestableQuota` returns `2+2+0=4`. And cohort usage is `2`.
  Then, `available=4-2=2`, which is less than `3` that the workload requests.
  
  But the workload actually fits.

### Review by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) (commented) — 2024-01-17T08:07:34Z

  That's true, this is because not all the used quota are lended, maybe we can add a new field named like **lendUsage**, it's the sum of all the lending usages. For example, for each cq except self, if the used quota is less or equal to the guaranteed quota , the lend usage is 0, else, the lend usage is `usedQuota - guaranteedQuota`. 
  
  Then maybe we no longer need the cohort.Usage anymore, let's see. WDYT?

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:548** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-23T16:12:24Z
```diff
@@ -493,3 +516,50 @@ func resetUsage(lqUsage FlavorResourceQuantities, cqUsage FlavorResourceQuantiti
 func workloadBelongsToLocalQueue(wl *kueue.Workload, q *kueue.LocalQueue) bool {
 	return wl.Namespace == q.Namespace && wl.Spec.QueueName == q.Name
 }
+
+// RequestableCohortQuota recalculates cohort.RequestableResources when LendingLimit enabled,
+// because when borrowing from the cohort, need to count cq's own nominal quota in.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, RequestableResources only contains the sum of
+	// all CQs' LendingLimit, so we need to add the guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
```

  ```suggestion
  	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil || c.GuaranteeQuota[fName] == nil {
  		return 0
  	}
  ```
  
  for simplify

```diff
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, RequestableResources only contains the sum of
+	// all CQs' LendingLimit, so we need to add the guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	return c.GuaranteedQuota[fName][rName]
+}
+
+// CohortUsage recalculates cohort.Usage when LendingLimit enabled,
+// it represents the quota cq is using over its GuaranteedQuota.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) CohortUsage(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	cohortUsage := c.Cohort.Usage[fName][rName]
```

  Plz add defender here:
  ```
  if c.Cohort.Usage == nil || c.Cohot.Usage[fName] == nil {
      return 0
  }
  ```

- **apis/kueue/v1beta1/clusterqueue_types.go:212** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-24T06:21:17Z
```diff
@@ -201,6 +201,16 @@ type ResourceQuota struct {
 	// borrowingLimit must be null if spec.cohort is empty.
 	// +optional
 	BorrowingLimit *resource.Quantity `json:"borrowingLimit,omitempty"`
+
+	// lendingLimit is the maximum amount of unused quota for the [flavor, resource]
+	// combination that this ClusterQueue can lend to other ClusterQueues in the same cohort.
+	// In total, at a given time, ClusterQueue reserves for its exclusive use
+	// a quantity of quota equals to nominalQuota - lendingLimit.
+	// If null, it means that there is no lending limit.
+	// If not null, it must be non-negative.
+	// lendingLimit must be null if spec.cohort is empty.
```

  ```suggestion
  	// lendingLimit must be null if spec.cohort is empty.
  	// It's alpha now controlled by feature gate LendingLimit, disabled by default.
  ```

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:558** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-24T06:41:44Z
```diff
@@ -493,3 +516,50 @@ func resetUsage(lqUsage FlavorResourceQuantities, cqUsage FlavorResourceQuantiti
 func workloadBelongsToLocalQueue(wl *kueue.Workload, q *kueue.LocalQueue) bool {
 	return wl.Namespace == q.Namespace && wl.Spec.QueueName == q.Name
 }
+
+// RequestableCohortQuota recalculates cohort.RequestableResources when LendingLimit enabled,
+// because when borrowing from the cohort, need to count cq's own nominal quota in.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, RequestableResources only contains the sum of
+	// all CQs' LendingLimit, so we need to add the guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	return c.GuaranteedQuota[fName][rName]
+}
+
+// CohortUsage recalculates cohort.Usage when LendingLimit enabled,
+// it represents the quota cq is using over its GuaranteedQuota.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) CohortUsage(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	cohortUsage := c.Cohort.Usage[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, all CQs' GuaranteedQuota are reserved for itself, cannot be borrowed
+	// by other CQs in the cohort, so we need to remove the guaranteed resources from Cohort.Usage.
+	cohortUsage -= c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
```

  This is not right, because the cohortUsage you accumulated is the sum of all the clusterQueues, minus self guaranteed resource is not enough. You should process this for each clusterQueue.

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:560** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-24T15:31:07Z
```diff
@@ -493,3 +515,54 @@ func resetUsage(lqUsage FlavorResourceQuantities, cqUsage FlavorResourceQuantiti
 func workloadBelongsToLocalQueue(wl *kueue.Workload, q *kueue.LocalQueue) bool {
 	return wl.Namespace == q.Namespace && wl.Spec.QueueName == q.Name
 }
+
+// RequestableCohortQuota returns the total available quota by the flavor and resource name in the cohort.
+// LendingLimit will also be counted here if feature LendingLimit enabled.
+// Please note that for different clusterQueues, the requestable quota is different,
+// they should be calculated dynamically.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources == nil || c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, cohort.requestableResource accumulated the lendingLimit if not null
+	// rather than the flavor's quota, then the total available quota should include its own guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil || c.GuaranteedQuota[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	return c.GuaranteedQuota[fName][rName]
+}
+
+// UsedCohortQuota recalculates cohort.Usage when LendingLimit enabled,
+// it represents the quota cq is using over its GuaranteedQuota.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) UsedCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.Usage == nil || c.Cohort.Usage[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}

+	cohortUsage := c.Cohort.Usage[fName][rName]
```

```diff
+	// need to count the cqUsage in, otherwise need to count the ReservedQuota in.
```

```diff
 			},
+		},
+		"missing flavor": {
 			request: FlavorResourceQuantities{
 				"f2": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
 					corev1.ResourceCPU:    1,
 					corev1.ResourceMemory: 1,
 				},
 			},
 			wantFit: false,
-		},
-		"missing resource": {
-			c: &Cohort{
-				Name: "C",
-				RequestableResources: FlavorResourceQuantities{
-					"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
-						corev1.ResourceCPU: 5,
+			cq: &ClusterQueue{
+				Name: "CQ",
+				Cohort: &Cohort{
+					Name: "C",
+					RequestableResources: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							corev1.ResourceCPU:    5,
+							corev1.ResourceMemory: 5,
+						},
 					},
-				},
-				Usage: FlavorResourceQuantities{
-					"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
-						corev1.ResourceCPU: 3,
+					Usage: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							corev1.ResourceCPU:    5,
+							corev1.ResourceMemory: 5,
+						},
 					},
 				},
+				ResourceGroups: nil,
 			},
+		},
+		"missing resource": {
 			request: FlavorResourceQuantities{
 				"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
 					corev1.ResourceCPU:    1,
 					corev1.ResourceMemory: 1,
 				},
 			},
 			wantFit: false,
+			cq: &ClusterQueue{
+				Name: "CQ",
+				Cohort: &Cohort{
+					Name: "C",
+					RequestableResources: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							corev1.ResourceCPU: 5,
+						},
+					},
+					Usage: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							corev1.ResourceCPU: 3,
+						},
+					},
+				},
+				ResourceGroups: nil,
+			},
+		},
+		"lendingLimit enabled can't fit": {
+			request: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+				"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+					corev1.ResourceCPU: 3,
+				},
+			},
+			wantFit: false,
+			cq: &ClusterQueue{
+				Name: "CQ-A",
+				Cohort: &Cohort{
+					Name: "C",
+					RequestableResources: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							// CQ-A has 2 nominal cpu, CQ-B has 3 nominal cpu and 2 lendingLimit,
+							// so when lendingLimit enabled, the cohort's RequestableResources is 4 cpu.
+							corev1.ResourceCPU: 4,
+						},
+					},
+					Usage: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							corev1.ResourceCPU: 2,
+						},
+					},
+				},
+				GuaranteedQuota: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+					"f1": {
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: 0,
+					},
+				},
+			},
+			enableLendingLimit: true,
+		},
+		"lendingLimit enabled can fit": {
+			request: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+				"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+					corev1.ResourceCPU: 3,
+				},
+			},
+			wantFit: true,
+			cq: &ClusterQueue{
+				Name: "CQ-A",
+				Cohort: &Cohort{
+					Name: "C",
+					RequestableResources: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							// CQ-A has 2 nominal cpu, CQ-B has 3 nominal cpu and 2 lendingLimit,
+							// so when lendingLimit enabled, the cohort's RequestableResources is 4 cpu.
+							corev1.ResourceCPU: 4,
+						},
+					},
+					Usage: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+						"f1": map[corev1.ResourceName]int64{
+							// CQ-B has admitted a workload with 2 cpus, but with 1 GuaranteedQuota,
+							// so when lendingLimit enabled, Cohort.Usage should be 2 - 1 = 1.
+							corev1.ResourceCPU: 1,
+						},
+					},
+				},
+				GuaranteedQuota: FlavorResourceQuantities{
+					"f1": {
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: 0,
```

  I think the guaranteedQuota now should be greater than 0, than we can cover different scenarios. That's say we should refactor these tests.

```diff
+	ginkgo.When("Using cohorts for fair-sharing when LendingLimit enabled", func() {
+		var (
+			prodCQ *kueue.ClusterQueue
+			devCQ  *kueue.ClusterQueue
+		)
+
+		ginkgo.BeforeEach(func() {
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, onDemandFlavor)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, spotTaintedFlavor)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, spotUntaintedFlavor)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+			gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+			util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, prodCQ, true)
+			if devCQ != nil {
+				util.ExpectClusterQueueToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, devCQ, true)
+			}
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, onDemandFlavor, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, spotTaintedFlavor, true)
+			util.ExpectResourceFlavorToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, spotUntaintedFlavor, true)
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should admit workloads using borrowed ClusterQueue", func() {
+			prodCQ = testing.MakeClusterQueue("prod-cq").
+				Cohort("all").
+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("spot-tainted").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5", "0").Obj(),
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("on-demand").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5", "", "1").Obj(),
+				).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, prodCQ)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			queue := testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(prodCQ.Name).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, queue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			ginkgo.By("checking a no-fit workload does not get admitted")
+			wl := testing.MakeWorkload("wl", ns.Name).Queue(queue.Name).
+				Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "10").Toleration(spotToleration).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, wl)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			util.ExpectWorkloadsToBePending(ctx, k8sClient, wl)
+			util.ExpectPendingWorkloadsMetric(prodCQ, 0, 1)
+			util.ExpectReservingActiveWorkloadsMetric(prodCQ, 0)
+			util.ExpectAdmittedWorkloadsTotalMetric(prodCQ, 0)
+
+			ginkgo.By("checking the workload gets admitted when a fallback ClusterQueue gets added")
+			fallbackClusterQueue := testing.MakeClusterQueue("fallback-cq").
+				Cohort(prodCQ.Spec.Cohort).
+				ResourceGroup(
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("spot-tainted").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5").Obj(), // prod-cq can't borrow this due to its borrowingLimit
+					*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("on-demand").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5", "", "5").Obj(),
```

```diff
+			prodCQ = testing.MakeClusterQueue("prod-cq").
+				Cohort("all").
+				ResourceGroup(*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("on-demand").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5", "10", "5").Obj()).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, prodCQ)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			devCQ = testing.MakeClusterQueue("dev-cq").
+				Cohort("all").
+				ResourceGroup(*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("on-demand").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5", "10", "5").Obj()).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, devCQ)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			prodQueue := testing.MakeLocalQueue("prod-queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(prodCQ.Name).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, prodQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			devQueue := testing.MakeLocalQueue("dev-queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(devCQ.Name).Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, devQueue)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			wl1 := testing.MakeWorkload("wl-1", ns.Name).Queue(prodQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "11").Obj()
+			wl2 := testing.MakeWorkload("wl-2", ns.Name).Queue(devQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "11").Obj()
+
+			ginkgo.By("Creating two workloads")
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, wl1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, wl2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			util.ExpectWorkloadsToBePending(ctx, k8sClient, wl1, wl2)
+			util.ExpectPendingWorkloadsMetric(prodCQ, 0, 1)
+			util.ExpectPendingWorkloadsMetric(devCQ, 0, 1)
+			util.ExpectReservingActiveWorkloadsMetric(prodCQ, 0)
+			util.ExpectReservingActiveWorkloadsMetric(devCQ, 0)
+			util.ExpectAdmittedWorkloadsTotalMetric(prodCQ, 0)
+			util.ExpectAdmittedWorkloadsTotalMetric(devCQ, 0)
+
+			// Delay cluster queue creation to make sure workloads are in the same
+			// scheduling cycle.
+			testCQ := testing.MakeClusterQueue("test-cq").
+				Cohort("all").
+				ResourceGroup(*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas("on-demand").Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "15", "0", "12").Obj()).
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, testCQ)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			defer func() {
+				gomega.Expect(util.DeleteClusterQueue(ctx, k8sClient, testCQ)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			}()
+
+			util.ExpectWorkloadsToHaveQuotaReservation(ctx, k8sClient, prodCQ.Name, wl1)
+			util.ExpectWorkloadsToHaveQuotaReservation(ctx, k8sClient, devCQ.Name, wl2)
+			util.ExpectPendingWorkloadsMetric(prodCQ, 0, 0)
+			util.ExpectPendingWorkloadsMetric(devCQ, 0, 0)
+			util.ExpectReservingActiveWorkloadsMetric(prodCQ, 1)
+			util.ExpectReservingActiveWorkloadsMetric(devCQ, 1)
+			util.ExpectAdmittedWorkloadsTotalMetric(prodCQ, 1)
+			util.ExpectAdmittedWorkloadsTotalMetric(devCQ, 1)
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should try next flavor instead of borrowing", func() {
```

  Let remove this test since we already have similar one on the above, instead let's add a new test case which will cover the cache usage/requestableQuota. it generally look like:
  1. create a workload, it will be admitted.
  2. create another workload, unadmitted because of the lendingLimit
  3. update the lendingLimit
  4. the latter workload admitted.
  
  Or you can combine this with the first testcase.

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:559** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-29T10:23:24Z
```diff
@@ -493,3 +520,57 @@ func resetUsage(lqUsage FlavorResourceQuantities, cqUsage FlavorResourceQuantiti
 func workloadBelongsToLocalQueue(wl *kueue.Workload, q *kueue.LocalQueue) bool {
 	return wl.Namespace == q.Namespace && wl.Spec.QueueName == q.Name
 }
+
+// RequestableCohortQuota returns the total available quota by the flavor and resource name in the cohort.
+// LendingLimit will also be counted here if feature LendingLimit enabled.
+// Please note that for different clusterQueues, the requestable quota is different,
+// they should be calculated dynamically.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources == nil || c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, cohort.requestableResource accumulated the lendingLimit if not null
+	// rather than the flavor's quota, then the total available quota should include its own guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil || c.GuaranteedQuota[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	return c.GuaranteedQuota[fName][rName]
+}
+
+// UsedCohortQuota returns the used quota by the flavor and resource name in the cohort.
+// Note that when LendingLimit enabled, the usage is not equal to the total used quota but the one
+// minus the guaranteed resources, this is only for judging whether workloads fit in the cohort.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) UsedCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.Usage == nil || c.Cohort.Usage[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+
+	// Similar to cohort.RequestableResources, we accumulate the lendingLimit rather than the quota,
```

  Remove this, we have explain the reason below. sorry for that.

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:562** by [@kerthcet](https://github.com/kerthcet) — 2024-01-29T10:24:51Z
```diff
@@ -493,3 +520,57 @@ func resetUsage(lqUsage FlavorResourceQuantities, cqUsage FlavorResourceQuantiti
 func workloadBelongsToLocalQueue(wl *kueue.Workload, q *kueue.LocalQueue) bool {
 	return wl.Namespace == q.Namespace && wl.Spec.QueueName == q.Name
 }
+
+// RequestableCohortQuota returns the total available quota by the flavor and resource name in the cohort.
+// LendingLimit will also be counted here if feature LendingLimit enabled.
+// Please note that for different clusterQueues, the requestable quota is different,
+// they should be calculated dynamically.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources == nil || c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, cohort.requestableResource accumulated the lendingLimit if not null
+	// rather than the flavor's quota, then the total available quota should include its own guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if !features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
+		return 0
+	}
+	if c.GuaranteedQuota == nil || c.GuaranteedQuota[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	return c.GuaranteedQuota[fName][rName]
+}
+
+// UsedCohortQuota returns the used quota by the flavor and resource name in the cohort.
+// Note that when LendingLimit enabled, the usage is not equal to the total used quota but the one
+// minus the guaranteed resources, this is only for judging whether workloads fit in the cohort.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) UsedCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.Usage == nil || c.Cohort.Usage[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+
+	// Similar to cohort.RequestableResources, we accumulate the lendingLimit rather than the quota,
+	// here we should add the cqUsage as well for that part have not been accumulated.
+	cohortUsage := c.Cohort.Usage[fName][rName]
+	cqUsage := c.Usage[fName][rName]
```

  Remove this, lets add `c.Usage[fName][rName] directly in L569, or no longer need to calculate when feature disabled.

```diff
+				Priority(lowPriority).
+				Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5").
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, aBestEffortLowWl)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			ginkgo.By("Await for the a-best-effort-low workload to be admitted")
+			util.ExpectWorkloadToBeAdmittedAs(ctx, k8sClient, aBestEffortLowWl,
+				testing.MakeAdmission(aBestEffortCQ.Name).Assignment(corev1.ResourceCPU, "one", "5").Obj(),
+			)
+
+			ginkgo.By("Create a high priority workload (above MaxPriorityThreshold) which requires borrowing")
+			bStandardWl := testing.MakeWorkload("b-standard-high", ns.Name).
+				Queue(bStandardLQ.Name).
+				Priority(highPriority).
+				Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "5").
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, bStandardWl)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			ginkgo.By("Await for the b-standard-high workload to be admitted")
+			util.ExpectWorkloadToBeAdmittedAs(ctx, k8sClient, bStandardWl,
+				testing.MakeAdmission(bStandardCQ.Name).Assignment(corev1.ResourceCPU, "one", "5").Obj(),
+			)
+
+			ginkgo.By("Create the a-standard-very-high workload")
+			aStandardVeryHighWl := testing.MakeWorkload("a-standard-very-high", ns.Name).
+				Queue(aStandardLQ.Name).
+				Priority(veryHighPriority).
+				Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "6").
+				Obj()
+			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, aStandardVeryHighWl)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+
+			ginkgo.By("Finish eviction fo the a-best-effort-low workload")
```

  ```suggestion
  			ginkgo.By("Finish eviction for the a-best-effort-low workload")
  ```

- **apis/kueue/v1beta1/clusterqueue_types.go:212** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2024-02-06T20:04:11Z
```diff
@@ -201,6 +201,17 @@ type ResourceQuota struct {
 	// borrowingLimit must be null if spec.cohort is empty.
 	// +optional
 	BorrowingLimit *resource.Quantity `json:"borrowingLimit,omitempty"`
+
+	// lendingLimit is the maximum amount of unused quota for the [flavor, resource]
+	// combination that this ClusterQueue can lend to other ClusterQueues in the same cohort.
+	// In total, at a given time, ClusterQueue reserves for its exclusive use
+	// a quantity of quota equals to nominalQuota - lendingLimit.
+	// If null, it means that there is no lending limit.
+	// If not null, it must be non-negative.
+	// lendingLimit must be null if spec.cohort is empty.
+	// It's alpha now controlled by feature gate LendingLimit, disabled by default.
```

  ```suggestion
  	// This field is in alpha stage. To be able to use this field, enable the feature gate LendingLimit, which is disabled by default.
  ```

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:541** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2024-02-06T20:30:19Z
```diff
@@ -493,3 +520,55 @@ func resetUsage(lqUsage FlavorResourceQuantities, cqUsage FlavorResourceQuantiti
 func workloadBelongsToLocalQueue(wl *kueue.Workload, q *kueue.LocalQueue) bool {
 	return wl.Namespace == q.Namespace && wl.Spec.QueueName == q.Name
 }
+
+// RequestableCohortQuota returns the total available quota by the flavor and resource name in the cohort.
+// LendingLimit will also be counted here if feature LendingLimit enabled.
+// Please note that for different clusterQueues, the requestable quota is different,
+// they should be calculated dynamically.
+func (c *ClusterQueue) RequestableCohortQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
+	if c.Cohort.RequestableResources == nil || c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName] == nil {
+		return 0
+	}
+	requestableCohortQuota := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[fName][rName]
+
+	// When feature LendingLimit enabled, cohort.requestableResource accumulated the lendingLimit if not null
+	// rather than the flavor's quota, then the total available quota should include its own guaranteed resources.
+	requestableCohortQuota += c.ReservedQuota(fName, rName)
+
+	return requestableCohortQuota
+}
+
+func (c *ClusterQueue) ReservedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
```

  ```suggestion
  func (c *ClusterQueue) guaranteedQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.ResourceName) (val int64) {
  ```

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:133** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2024-02-06T20:39:33Z
```diff
@@ -120,12 +125,11 @@ func newCohort(name string, size int) *Cohort {
 	}
 }
 
-func (c *Cohort) CanFit(q FlavorResourceQuantities) bool {
+func (c *ClusterQueue) FitInCohort(q FlavorResourceQuantities) bool {
 	for flavor, qResources := range q {
-		if cohortResources, flavorFound := c.RequestableResources[flavor]; flavorFound {
-			cohortUsage := c.Usage[flavor]
+		if _, flavorFound := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[flavor]; flavorFound {
 			for resource, value := range qResources {
-				available := cohortResources[resource] - cohortUsage[resource]
+				available := c.RequestableCohortQuota(flavor, resource) - c.UsedCohortQuota(flavor, resource)
```

  Also, an alternative implementation is as follows:
  
  1. `cohort.RequestableResources` only contains the sum of lendingLimits (same as your approach).
  2. `cohort.Usage` only contains the usage within the `RequestableResources` as defined in 1 (same as your approach).
  3. When evaluating a workload admission, we calculate: `excess := workload.request-guaranteed`. The workload fits if `cohort.Usage+excess <= cohort.RequestableResources`.
  
  Both implementations are equivalent, but I think this is easier to document and follow along.




  I'm not convinced that this formula works.

### Review by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) (commented) — 2024-02-07T08:42:50Z

- **pkg/scheduler/flavorassigner/flavorassigner.go:578** by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2024-02-07T08:42:50Z
```diff
@@ -572,7 +572,7 @@ func fitsResourceQuota(fName kueue.ResourceFlavorReference, rName corev1.Resourc
 
 	cohortUsed := used
 	if cq.Cohort != nil {
-		cohortUsed = cq.Cohort.Usage[fName][rName]
+		cohortUsed = cq.UsedCohortQuota(fName, rName)
 	}
 
 	lack := cohortUsed + val - cohortAvailable
```

  According to our [design](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1385/files#diff-6f7611f9158b1c0d7bbc28edd666c01b781e7f074243a85e8d3b9ab95e6bf529), when we [accumulate](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1385/files#diff-bd8411463d27f0b9477a855409c5133c437d8cae368eeff5c2e5957f26c23507R189-R198) `cohort.Usage` in snapshot, we will substract the guaranteedQuota, only count how much quota used in `cohort.RequestableResources`(sum of `LendingLimit`).
  And in function `UsedCohortQuota`, we count the `cqUsage` in when the cq is not using all its guaranteedQuota(otherwise count the guaranteedQuota in).

### Review by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) (commented) — 2024-02-08T03:23:42Z

- **pkg/cache/clusterqueue.go:133** by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2024-02-08T03:23:42Z
```diff
@@ -120,12 +125,11 @@ func newCohort(name string, size int) *Cohort {
 	}
 }
 
-func (c *Cohort) CanFit(q FlavorResourceQuantities) bool {
+func (c *ClusterQueue) FitInCohort(q FlavorResourceQuantities) bool {
 	for flavor, qResources := range q {
-		if cohortResources, flavorFound := c.RequestableResources[flavor]; flavorFound {
-			cohortUsage := c.Usage[flavor]
+		if _, flavorFound := c.Cohort.RequestableResources[flavor]; flavorFound {
 			for resource, value := range qResources {
-				available := cohortResources[resource] - cohortUsage[resource]
+				available := c.RequestableCohortQuota(flavor, resource) - c.UsedCohortQuota(flavor, resource)
```

  > I would prefer we call the feature gate here, preserving the old code.
  
  We can change this part like this:
  ```
  for flavor, qResources := range q {
  	if cohortResources, flavorFound := c.RequestableResources[flavor]; flavorFound {
  		cohortUsage := c.Usage[flavor]
  		for resource, value := range qResources {
  			available := cohortResources[resource] - cohortUsage[resource]
  			if features.Enabled(features.LendingLimit) {
  				available = c.RequestableCohortQuota(flavor, resource) - c.UsedCohortQuota(flavor, resource)
  			}
  ```
  But since we already have featureGates inside of `c.RequestableCohortQuota` and `c.UsedCohortQuota`([RequestableCohortQuota](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1385/files#diff-441da8393964615cf5b020d0afb9199588e157e50718e83b527788eb679391ecR537), [guaranteedQuota](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1385/files#diff-441da8393964615cf5b020d0afb9199588e157e50718e83b527788eb679391ecR543), [UsedCohortQuota](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1385/files#diff-441da8393964615cf5b020d0afb9199588e157e50718e83b527788eb679391ecR565)), is it still necessary to add featureGates here?

  > But since we already have featureGates inside of c.RequestableCohortQuota and c.UsedCohortQuota(RequestableCohortQuota, guaranteedQuota, UsedCohortQuota), is it still necessary to add featureGates here?
  
  The fact that the usage of the feature gate is scattered among multiple functions makes it hard to visually verify if the old behavior is preserved. It's generally a good practice to use feature gates in a coarse manner.
  
  You could actually remove the feature gate checks from the new functions and check the feature gate in the flavorassigner code as well.

### Review by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) (commented) — 2024-02-21T14:47:58Z

- **pkg/cache/snapshot.go:192** by [@B1F030](https://github.com/B1F030) — 2024-02-21T14:47:58Z
```diff
@@ -173,6 +187,13 @@ func (c *ClusterQueue) accumulateResources(cohort *Cohort) {
 			cohort.Usage[fName] = used
 		}
 		for res, val := range resUsages {
+			// Similar to cohort.RequestableResources, we accumulate the usage above the guaranteed resources,
+			// here we should remove the guaranteed quota as well for that part can not be borrowed.
+			val -= c.guaranteedQuota(fName, res)
```

  > The logic is a bit hard to follow, so I am not sure if preemption is broken. But, semantically, the calculations of Add/Remove Workload are now wrong, because they don't consider the guaranteed quotas.
  
  We consider the guaranteed quotas in function `workloadFits` before we decide whether to `AddWorkload` or not(based on `fits: bool`). In [pkg/scheduler/preemption/preemption.go](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/main/pkg/scheduler/preemption/preemption.go#L378):
  when cohort is nil, means feature LendingLimit cannot be enabled, using the original logic;
  when cohort is not nil, go into function `cq.UsedCohortQuota` and `cq.RequestableCohortQuota`, consider the featureGate and the guaranteed quotas.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2024-02-21T15:48:16Z

- **pkg/cache/snapshot.go:192** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2024-02-21T15:48:16Z
```diff
@@ -173,6 +187,13 @@ func (c *ClusterQueue) accumulateResources(cohort *Cohort) {
 			cohort.Usage[fName] = used
 		}
 		for res, val := range resUsages {
+			// Similar to cohort.RequestableResources, we accumulate the usage above the guaranteed resources,
+			// here we should remove the guaranteed quota as well for that part can not be borrowed.
+			val -= c.guaranteedQuota(fName, res)
```

  Yes, I understand that `workloadFits` considers the guaranteed quotas. However, after we call `RemoveWorkload`, the cohort usage is semantically wrong (because this function doesn't consider guaranteed quotas). So I'm not convinced that the next call to `workloadFits` would be correct.
